 Let me tell you, amid opposition from the opposition, the government on Friday introduced a bill in the Lok Sabha to immediately ban triple talaq and make this practice a punishable offense under the Indian Penal Code
 vipaksh ne aarope lagaaya he ki yah muslim pariwaron ko nuksaan pahunchayegaa or yah vidheyak bhedbhaavpurn he
 As Union Law and Justice Minister Ravi Shankar Prasad introduced the Muslim Women (protection of Marriage Rights) Bill, 2019 in the Lok Sabha to ban triple talaq, opposition members demanded that all mps of political parties be included on it
 Extensive discussions should be held
 186 saansadon ne vidheyak ke paksh main matdaan kiya, vahiin 74 saansadon ne iske khilaaf matdaan kiya
 Presenting this, Union Minister Ravi Shankar Prasad said that people chose the government to make laws and it is their duty to do so

 majlis-e-ittehadul Muslimeen (MIM) president Asaduddin Owaisi demanded a division of the vote during its presentation

 The woman's husband will be jailed for three years for uttering the three talaqs immediately
 isse mahila par boj padegaa
 ' vaidic kaal pracheen bhartiya samskruti kaa ek kaal khand he
 Vedas were composed during that time
 hadappa samskruti ke patan ke baad bharat main ek nai sabhyataa kaa aavirbhaav hua
 Based on Vedas, the source of information of this civilization, it was named Vedic Civilization
 (1)vaidic kaal kaa vibhaajan do bhaagon rigvaidic kaal- 1500-1000 i
 e or uttar vaidic kaal- 1000-600 i
 e main kiya gaya he
 (2) Arya was first settled in Punjab and Afghanistan
 maxmooler ne aaryon kaa nivas sthaan madhya asia ko mana he
 The civilization built by the Aryans is called the Vedic civilization
 (3)aaryon dwaara viksit sabhyataa gramin sabhyataa thi
 The leader of the Rig Vedic Gods, the Godhead of God, the God of Rain and the God of Rain, the God of the Earth and the Creator of the Sun, the God of the sea, the regulator and ruler of the world, the symbol of truth, the God of change and day and night, the God of the most exalted and the deity of God God-godman-god Patrons w god of palnkrtamrutaandhi-storm (4) Aryan language was Sanskrit
 (5)aaryon kii prashasnic ikai in paanch bhaagon main banty thi: (i) kul (ii) gram (iii) vish (iv) jan (iv) raashtra
 (6) Monarchical system was prevalent in Vedic period
 (7)gram ke mukhiya gramini or vish kaa pradhan vishapati kehalaata tha
 The ruler of Jana was called Rajan
 rajdhikariyon main purohit or senaanee pramukh the
 (8) The head of the rule was the king
 raja vanshanugat to hota tha lekin janata use hataa sakati thi
 He was not the head of the region but was the head of the particular people
 (9)raja yuddh kaa netritvkarta tha
 He did not have the right to collect tax
 janata apni ichha se jo detii thi, raja usee se kharch chalaata tha
 (10) The administrative support of the king was done by priests and fighters 12 Ratnins
 charaagaah ke pradhan ko vajrapati or ladaaku dalon ke pradhan ko gramini kaha jaataa tha
 (11) 12 Ratnins were as follows: Purohit- King's chief counselor, Fighter- Army chief, Rural- village soldier, Mahishi- King's wife, Soot- Raja's charioteer, Kshatri- Pratihara, Collected- Treasurer, Bhagududh - Tax collecting officer, Akshavap - Accountant, Govikrit - Forest officer, Palagal - Friend of the king
 (12)purup, durgpati or sparsh, janata kii gatividhiyon ko dekhne vaale guptchar hote the
 (13) Vajapati-pathar used to possess land
 (14)ugr-aparaadhiyon ko pakadaney kaa kaary karata tha
 (15) The Sabha and the Committee were an advisory body to the king
 (16)sabha shreshth or sambhraat logon kii sanstha thi, jabaki samiti saamaanya janata kaa pratinidhitiv karti thi or vidath sabase pracheen sanstha thi
 The Rig Veda is mentioned 122 times with the highest Vidath
 (17)vidath main stri or purush donon sammalit hote the
 Social functions such as welcoming of newlyweds, religious rituals were done in the Vidath
 (18)atharvaveda main sabha or samiti ko prajapati kii do putriyaan kaha gaya he
 The important function of the committee was to elect the king
 samiti kaa pradhan ishan yaa pati kehalaata tha
 (19) There were different experts from different fields
 hotri- rugveda kaa paath karne vaala, udagatri- samaveda kii richaaon kaa gaan karne vaala, adhvaryu- yajurveda kaa paath karne vaala or rivindh- sampurna yagyon kii dekh-rekh karne vaala
 (20) In battle the clan was headed by the king, the word gavishtha of war was used which means search for cows
 (21)dasarajya yuddh kaa ullekh rugveda ke saatven mandal main he, yah yuddh raavi nadi ke tat par sudas or das janon ke bich ladaa gaya tha
 In which Sudas won
 (22)rigvaidic samaaj brahman, kshatriya, vaisya or shudra main vibhajit tha
 This division was based on business
 rugveda ke 10wein mandal main kaha gaya he ki brahman param purush ke mukh se, kshatriya unki bhujaaon se, vaisya unki jaanghon se or shudra unke pairon se utpann hue hai
 The major philosophy and its originator was the enlightenment; (24)bhikhaariyon or krishi daason kaa astitv nahin tha
 The unit of property was the cow which was also the medium of exchange
 sarathi or badhai samudaay ko vishesh sammaan praapt tha
 (25) The Aryan society was patriarchal
 samaaj kii sabase choti ikai parivaar thi jiskaa mukhiya pita hota tha jise kulp kehete the
 (26) Women used to participate in yagna work with their husbands during this period
 (27)bal vivaah or pardaapratha kaa prachlan is kaal main nahin tha
 (28) The widow could marry her husband's younger brother
 vidhwaa vivaah, mahilaon kaa upanayan sanskaar, niyog gandharv or antarjaatiy vivaah prachlit tha
 (29) Women could study
 rugveda main ghosha, apala, vishwaas jaisi vidhushi mahilaon ko varnan he
 (30) a woman who remained unmarried throughout her life was called Amaju
 (31)aaryon kaa mukhya peya somras tha
 Which was made from vegetation
 (32)arya teen tarah ke kapadon kaa istemaal karte the
 (i) Habitat (ii) Domicile (iii) Temperate (iv) Clothing worn inside was called Nivi
 sangeet, rathdaud, ghuddaud aaryon ke manoranjan ke saadhan the
 (33) The main occupation of the Aryans was farming and animal husbandry
 (34)gaay ko na maare jane pashu kii shrenee main rakhaa gaya tha
 (35) The person who killed or injured the cow was sentenced to death or deportation
 rigvedikkaleen nadiyanpracheen namedhunik namkrubhakurramkubhakabulavitastajhelmaskinichinavaparushaniravishtudristaljavipashavyasasdaniragandkadrusaddhatighagghargomalgomtisuvastuswath(36)aaryon kaa priy pashu ghoda or priy devtaa indra the
 (37) The metal discovered by the Aryans was iron
 (38)vyapaar ke dur-dur jane vaale vyakti ko pani kaha jaataa tha
 (39) The barter system existed in the transaction
 (40)rin dekar byaaj dene vaale ko soodakhor kaha jaataa tha
 (41) Of all the rivers, Saraswati was considered the most important and sacred river
 (42)uttaravaidic kaal main prajapati priy devtaa ban gaye the
 (43) In the later Vedic period the varna was determined on the basis of birth rather than occupation
 (44)uttaravaidic kaal main hal ko sira or hal rekha ko sita kaha jaataa tha
 (45) In the later Vedic period, Nishka and Shataman were units of Mudra
 (46)sankhya darshan bharat ke sabhi darshanon main sabase purana tha
 According to this, the basic elements are 25, of which the first element is nature
 (47)satyamev jayate, mundakopanishad se liya gaya he
 (48) The Gayatri mantra is addressed to a deity named Savita who is related to the Rigveda
 (49)uttar vaidic kaal main kaushambi nagar main pehali baar pakki eenton kaa istemaal hua tha
 (50) The epics are two - Mahabharata and Ramayana
 (51)mahabharat kaa purana naam jaisanhita he yah vishwa kaa sabase bada mahakavy he
 (52) In the first 'jabalopanishad', there is mention of the four ashrams Brahmacharya, Grihastha, Vanaprastha and Sannyas Ashram
 (53)gotra naamak sanstha kaa janm uttar vaidic kaal main hua
 (54) Among the metals in the Rigveda, copper or bronze is first mentioned
 ve sona or chaandi se bhi parichit the
 But iron is not mentioned in Rigveda

 Children forget everything while playing
 khilne ke dauraan na to unhen garmi lagati he or na hi thakaan hoti he lekin suraj kii garmi or taap unke liye khatarnaak sabit ho saktaa he
 On one hand there is weakness due to heat, on the other hand, the risk of getting many diseases also increases
 ab bachche hai to ham unhen khilne-kudane se roak nahin sakate par aap chahen to in upayon ko apanaakar aap apane bacchon ko surakshit rakh sakate hai
 Let's know how to save children from the heat of summer
 
 
 -garmi ke mausam main bacchon kii pachan shakti kamjor ho jaati he
 During this period, children are more susceptible to diarrhea, heat stroke, stomach irritation, vomiting, jaundice, typhoid
 isliye bacchon ke khanpan kaa puraa dhyaan rakhen or unhen halkaa, paushtik aahaar den
 Do it -khilne ke dauraan bachche sabakuch bhul jate hai ormausam kaa dhyaan die bina hi khelte rahete hai
 In such a situation, keep in mind that the child should not play during strong sunlight or sun
 shaam hone par hi bachche ko baahar jane den
 During the day, ask him to play indoor games
 - garmiyon main shaam ke vakt machhar or keede kaaphi sakriy ho jate hai
 In such a situation, when the child is going to play, send him outside only by applying cream that provides protection from insects and mosquitoes
 -koshish karen ki baccha baahar kii koi cheez na khaae
 To prevent de-hydration, give children as much liquid as possible
 unhen ghar main hi bana zeus, nibu pani yaa phir nariyal pani pine ko den
 Buttermilk, fresh fruit juice, milk shake can also be given to the child
 iske alaava khiraa, kakadi or tarbooz bhi khaane ko de sakate hai
 There will be no shortage of water in the child's body due to their consumption
 - garmiyon ke dinon main bacchon ko din main do baar nahaane kii aadat dalawaaen
 Wear baby clothes only and change clothes daily
 kahin bhi baahar se aane par uske haath pair acchhee tarah se sabun se saaf karavaaen
 Doing so will reduce the risk of infection
 -mausam kaa dhyaan rakhte hue sard-garm kaa khyaal rakhen jaise, agar bachche dhoop main khelkar waapas aaen to cooler ke saamne na baithne den or turant hi thanda pani bhi na den
 - The risk of conjunctivitis in the summer season is also increased
 isliye thode-thode antaraal ke baad bacchon kii ankhen thande pani se dhulawaate rahen
 This will not cause dryness in the eyes of children
 - bacchon ko garmiyon main aksar ghamauriyon or sanbern kii samasya ho jaati he

 anbhavi ballebaaj kumaar sangakaara ke shandaar shatak or 'pinch heater' nuwan kulshekhara kii tufaani pari se srilanka ne england par saat wicket kii dhamaakedaar jeet darj karke isisi champions trophy main apni ummiido ko barkaraar rakhaa
 Sangakkara played an unbeaten 134-run knock, but Kulasekara's unbeaten 58 off 38 balls also played an important role in giving Sri Lanka the victory with 17 balls to spare
 in donon ne chauthe wicket ke liye 110 ran kii atoot saajhedaari kii
 Sangakkara had earlier added 92 for the second wicket with Tillakaratne Dilshan (44) and 85 for the third wicket with Mahela Jayawardene (42)
 srilanka ne 47
 Scored 297 runs for three wickets in 1 over
 isse pehle, england ne pehle ballebaaji kaa nyotaa milane par saat wicket par 293 ran kaa majboot score khadaa kiya tha

 unhone captain elistare cook (59) ke saath 83 or jo root (68) ke saath 87 ran kii saajhedaariyaan kin

 dilashaan ne shuruaati jhijak ke baad root kii lagaataar gedon par chaukaa or chakka lagaakar teji dikhaai
 Dilshan lost patience as he scored only six runs in three consecutive overs in the middle and gave an easy catch on long on off Swan
 sangakaara ne ek chor par tike rahakar score chalyman rakhaa
 New batsman Jayawardene soon set foot
 sangakaara kii tarah unhone bhi stuart broad ko nishane par rakhaa
 Sri Lanka lost the wicket of Jayawardene on the second ball of the batting powerplay
 unhone anderson kii gend baikfoot par jaakar pul kii, lekin use becoward squaire leg par kaich kar liya gaya
 Sri Lanka made the interesting, but right decision to replace him with Kulasekara
 srilanka ne ballebaaji powerple main 31 ran banaae or ek wicket ganvaaya
 Meanwhile, Sangakkara finished 15th in odis and his first century against England by taking a run on Tim Bresnan
 iske liye unhone 111 gend kheli tathaa aath chauke lagaae
 Kulasekara also soon did justice to his role as a pinch hitter
 bresanan par do chauke jadne ke baad unhone greem swaan par lagaataar do chakke lagaae
 He hit a six and then two fours on Broad to complete his third ODI half-century off just 30 balls
 sangakaara ne vijayi chaukaa jamaaya

 unhone 72 gendon par apana ardhashatak puraa kiya

 traat or root ne strike rotate karne kii ranneeti apanaai, jisase ran gati main teji ai

 tippaniyan England scored 37 runs in the batting powerplay and lost no wickets in the meantime
